# Marlin Processor Overview

This page lists all Marlin processors available in the Key4hep software stack,
collected from the active environment. Use the search box to filter by processor
name, package, or library. Click a package header to collapse or expand it; click
a processor name to reveal its parameters.

Total: **212 processors** across **20 packages**.

```{raw} html
      <div class="alg-card" data-name="CutOnGEANT4Bug" data-lib="" data-package="">
        <div class="alg-card-header">
          <span class="alg-name">CutOnGEANT4Bug</span>
          <span class="alg-card-right">
            <span class="alg-card-toggle">&#9658;</span>
          </span>
        </div>
        <div class="alg-card-body">
          <p class="alg-description">The output condition of this processor is true as long as no track has more than a factor of k more energy deposited in the calorimeter as its energy given by momentum and mass. This should cut out events where GEANT4 produces additional energy depositions. If at least one such a track is found the return value is false. Only tracks with an energy larger than eMin are taken into account.</p>
          <table class="alg-props-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Parameter</th>
                <th>Type</th>
                <th>Default</th>
                <th>Description</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><code>calibrCoeffECAL</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>33.0235 93.5682</code></td>
                <td>Calibration coefficients for ECAL</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>calibrCoeffHCAL</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>21.1963</code></td>
                <td>Calibration coefficients for HCAL</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>colNameRelationCaloHitToSimCaloHit</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>RelationCaloHit</code></td>
                <td>name of the LC Relation collection between Calorimeterhits and SimCalorimeterhits</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>colNameRelationTrackToMCP</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>TrueTrackToMCP</code></td>
                <td>name of the LC Relation collection between Tracks and MC particles</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>colNameTracks</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>Tracks</code></td>
                <td>name of the Track collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>eMin</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>minimal energy of tracks taken into account (in GeV)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>k</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>1.75</code></td>
                <td>if the track has more than k times its MC energy deposited the return value is set to false</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>

                <th>Type</th>

              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SelectionOffset</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>
                <td>Sets an offset m, so the Return Value of the mth event (and every nth before and after it) is set to true; default: 0</td>

                <td><code>int</code></td>

              </tr>

                <td><code>string</code></td>

              </tr>

                <td><code>HCalEndcapName</code></td>

              </tr>

                <td>Max R (mm) Extent for drawing Helix if UseTPCForLimitsOfHelix false</td>
              </tr>

                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>2500</code></td>

              </tr>

                <td><code>MCParticleEnergyCut</code></td>

              <tr>
                <td><code>UseColorForHelixTracks</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>

              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>UseTrackerExtentForLimitsOfHelix</code></td>

          <p class="alg-description">BeamCalClusterReco reproduces the beamstrahlung background for a given number of bunch-crossings NumberOfBX and puts the signal hits from the lcio input file on top of that, and then clustering is attempted.</p>

                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>-1</code></td>
                <td>Weighting constant to use in logarithmic weighting of hits, if negative energy weighting is used</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MCParticleCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>MCParticle</code></td>
                <td>MCParticle Collection Name, only needed and used to estimate efficiencies</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MaxPadDistance</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>1e+10</code></td>
                <td>Maximum Distance between primary tower and neighbours to put into one cluster</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MinimumTowerSize</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>4</code></td>
                <td>Minimum number of pads in a single tower to be considered for signal</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>NShowerCountingLayers</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>3</code></td>
                <td>How many layers are used for shower fitting</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>NumberOfBX</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>Number of Bunch Crossings of Background</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PrintThisEvent</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>-1</code></td>
                <td>Number of Event that should be printed to PDF File</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ReadoutName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>The Name of the DD4hep Readout belonging to the Detector the reconstruction is for, by default the name of the input collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>RecoClusterCollectionname</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>BCalClusters</code></td>
                <td>Name of the Reconstructed Cluster collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>RecoParticleCollectionname</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>BCalRecoParticle</code></td>
                <td>Name of the Reconstructed Particle collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SigmaCut</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>If not using ConstPadCuts, each pad SigmaCut*standardDeviation is considered for clusters</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>StartLookingInLayer</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>10</code></td>
                <td>Layer (inclusive) from which on we start looking for signal clusters</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>StartingRing</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>0 1 2</code></td>
                <td>Rings from which onwards the outside Thresholds are used</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SubClusterEnergyID</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>The ID where the SubClusterEnergy will be added: LumiCal=3, BeamCal=5 in DDPFOCreator.hh</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TowerChi2ndfLimit</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>Limit on square norm of tower energy chi2/ndf, where chi2 = (E_dep - E_bg)^2/sig^2. 			      Reasonable value for pregenerated bkg is 5., for parametrised is 2.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>UseChi2Selection</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Use Chi2 selection criteria to detect high energy electron in the signal.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>UseConstPadCuts</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>true</code></td>
                <td>Use the cuts for the pads specified in ETPad. If false, the standard deviation of each pad times the SigmaCut Factor is used, the first entry in ETPad is used as a minimum energy to consider a pad at all</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>

                <td><code>EcalEnergyMipConversion</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>140</code></td>
                <td>factor to convert between ECAL hit energy and MIP scale, for first layer</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>EcalPreClusterCollection</code></td>

              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ElectronClusterCollName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>GARLICElectronClusters</code></td>
                <td>Name of electron cluster collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ElectronTransTubeNSteps</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>3</code></td>
                <td>number of iterations for electron tube making</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ElectronTransTubeStepSize</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.75</code></td>
                <td>fraction of moliere radius with which to increment electron hit tube at each iteration</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ForwardTrackAngle</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.15</code></td>
                <td>Tracks with polar angle below this have less stringent cuts for electron finding (rad)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>GarlicConversionsPFOColName</code></td>

              </tr>

                <td><code>GarlicDebugCollections</code></td>

                <td>write out debug info collections to lcio file?</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>GarlicElectronsPFOColName</code></td>

              </tr>

              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MaxMergeDistEnDep</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>1.5</code></td>
                <td>maximum distance between clusters to consider merging: max(MaxMergeDistLowEn, MaxMergeDistLowEn + MaxMergeDistEnDep*log10(clusEn))</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MaxMergeDistLowEn</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>2</code></td>
                <td>maximum distance between clusters to consider merging: max(MaxMergeDistLowEn, MaxMergeDistLowEn + MaxMergeDistEnDep*log10(clusEn))</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MergeAbsoluteLargestDist</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>500</code></td>
                <td>don&#39;t consider merging two clusters if distance between cluster centres &gt; MergeAbsoluteLargestDist</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MergeEnergyDistFactor</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>120</code></td>
                <td>don&#39;t consider merging two clusters if E_min/E_max &gt; MergeEnergyDistFactor/(cl-cl dist **2) [cl-cl dist = transverse dist between clusters in mm]</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MergePi0MassLimit</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.1</code></td>
                <td>to veto merging 2 clusters, ask for their invariant mass to be consistent with a value &gt; MergePi0MassLimit @ 2 sigma, and that E_max/E_min &lt; MergePi0MaxEnergyImbalance</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MergePi0MaxEnergyImbalance</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>50</code></td>
                <td>to veto merging 2 clusters, ask for their invariant mass to be consistent with a value &gt; MergePi0MassLimit @ 2 sigma, and that E_max/E_min &lt; MergePi0MaxEnergyImbalance</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MergeRatioCut</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.25</code></td>
                <td>don&#39;t consider merging two clusters if E_min/E_max &gt; MergeRatioCut</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MoliereRadius</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>20</code></td>
                <td>assumed Moliere radius of ECAL (mm)</td>
              </tr>

            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Parameter</th>
                <th>Type</th>
                <th>Default</th>
                <th>Description</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ECM</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>500</code></td>
                <td>Center-of-Mass Energy in GeV</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>FitISR</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>0: Fit hypothesis without ISR   1: Fit hypothesis including ISR</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>FitOutputColection</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>FitReco</code></td>
                <td>Output Fit Colection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ISRPzMax</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>225</code></td>
                <td>Maximum possible energy for a single ISR photon</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>JetCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>Durham2Jets</code></td>
                <td>Name of the Jet collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MCParticleCollection</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>MCParticle</code></td>
                <td>Name of the MCParticle collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>NeutrinoCorrection</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>NuCorrect</code></td>
                <td>Collection of Corrected/Estimated neutrino energies from SemiLeptonic decays</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>NuEnergyCorrection</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>0: Fit hypothesis without ISR   1: Fit hypothesis including ISR</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SemiLeptonicDecays</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>Semi-Leptonic Decays Collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SigmaEnergyScaleFactor</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>Scale Factor t be applied to jet energy uncertainty</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>errene</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>1.2</code></td>
                <td>assumed energy resolution for jets as x/sqrt(E) - if 0, then parametrisation is used</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>errphi</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>0.1</code></td>
                <td>assumed phi resolution for jet axis</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>errtheta</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>0.1</code></td>
                <td>assumed theta resolution for jet axis</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>fitter</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>
                <td>0 = OPALFitter, 1 = NewFitter, 2 = NewtonFitter</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ievttrace</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>
                <td>number of individual event to be traced</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>outputFilename</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>name of output file</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>traceall</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>set true if every event should be traced</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>useErrorFlow</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>If true, use covariance matrix for energy uncertainty. Otherwise 1.2/sqrt(E)</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>

              <tr>
                <td><code>modeExtract</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>true</code></td>
                <td>Set true to extract the specified observables from the PFOs; if false you need to set the TTreeFileName instead; default: true.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>modeInfer</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Set true to infer the trained MVA with the specified observables to the PFOs; if true you need to provide the reference and weight files; default: false.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>modeTrain</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Set true to internally train an MVA with the specified observables from the PFOs; default: false.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>momLog</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>true</code></td>
                <td>For momentum bins: should the momentum bins be logarihtmic; default: true.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>momMax</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>100</code></td>
                <td>For momentum bins: maximum momentum cut / GeV; default: 100.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>momMin</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>For momentum bins: minimum momentum cut / GeV; default: 1.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>momNBins</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>12</code></td>
                <td>For momentum bins: number of momentum bins; default: 12.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>plotFolder</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>CPID_Plots</code></td>
                <td>Folder in which the automatic confusion matrix plots of inference will be put, is created if not already existing; if empty, no plots are created; default: CPID_Plots  [current working directory]</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>reffile</code></td>
                <td><code>StringVec</code></td>
                <td><code>Ref.txt</code></td>
                <td>Reference file(s), if only one file but several training models are specified the reference files are auto-numbered; default: {Ref.txt}.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>signalPDGs</code></td>
                <td><code>IntVec</code></td>
                <td><code>11 13 211 321 2212</code></td>
                <td>List of PDG numbers that are considered signal; default: {11,13,211,321,2212}.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>trainModelSpecs</code></td>
                <td><code>StringVec</code></td>
                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>List of training models; for each specify type:name or only type (then name=type); default: {}</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>trainingObservables</code></td>
                <td><code>StringVec</code></td>
                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>List of observables that should be used for traning; if empty, all observables from the specified algorithms + momabs + lambda are used; default: {}</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>

                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>Uniform</code></td>
                <td>Uniform polya or different polya per Asic</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PolyaRandomSeed</code></td>

                <td>The seed of the polya function</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PolyaWidthParameter</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>

                <td>Parameter for the Polya distribution used to simulate the induced charge distribution : related to the distribution width</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>RPC_PadSeparation</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>
                <td>distance in mm between two RPC pads : used if ChargeSplitterOption==Function or Erf</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SpreaderMapFile</code></td>

                <td><code></code></td>
                <td>Charge spreader map file</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>StepCellCenterMaxDistanceLayerDirection</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.0005</code></td>
                <td>Maximum distance (mm) between the Geant4 step position and the cell center, in the RPC width direction, to keep a step for digitization</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>StepLengthCut</code></td>

                <td><code>-1</code></td>

                <td><code>TimeCut</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>1.79769e+308</code></td>
                <td>Time cut</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>doThresholds</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>true</code></td>
                <td>Replace analog hit energy by value given in CalibrHCAL according to thresholds given in HCALThreshold</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>erfWeigth</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>Weigth for the different Erf functions</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>erfWidth</code></td>

                <td>Width values for the different Erf functions</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>functionRange</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>30</code></td>
                <td>maximal distance (in mm) at which a step can induce charge using the 2D function defined with functionFormula or when using ChargeSplitterOption==Erf</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>inputHitCollections</code></td>

      <div class="alg-card" data-name="TPCDigiProcessor" data-lib="MarlinReco" data-package="MarlinReco">
        <div class="alg-card-header">
          <span class="alg-name">TPCDigiProcessor</span>
          <span class="alg-card-right">
            <span class="alg-lib-badge">MarlinReco</span>
            <span class="alg-card-toggle">&#9658;</span>
          </span>
        </div>
        <div class="alg-card-body">
          <p class="alg-description">Produces TPC TrackerHit collection from SimTrackerHit collection, smeared in RPhi and Z. A search is made for adjacent hits on a pad row, if they are closer in z and r-phi than the steering parameters _doubleHitResRPhi (default value 2.0 mm) and _doubleHitResZ (default value 5.0 mm) they are considered to overlap. Clusters of hits smaller than _maxMerge (default value 3) are merged into a single tracker hit, with the position given as the average poision of the hits in phi and in z. Clusters which have _maxMerge hits or more are determined to be identifiable as multiple hits, and are not added to the tracker hit collection. This of course means that good hits caught up in a cluster of background hits will be lossed.</p>
          <table class="alg-props-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Parameter</th>
                <th>Type</th>
                <th>Default</th>
                <th>Description</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DiffusionCoeffRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.025</code></td>
                <td>R-Phi Diffusion Coefficent in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DiffusionCoeffZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.08</code></td>
                <td>Z Diffusion Coefficent in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DontEncodeSide</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>true</code></td>
                <td>Do not encode the side in the cellID of the TrackerHit</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DoubleHitResolutionRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>2</code></td>
                <td>Defines the minimum distance for two seperable hits in RPhi</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DoubleHitResolutionZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>Defines the minimum distance for two seperable hits in Z</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>HitSortingBinningRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>2</code></td>
                <td>Defines spatial slice in RP</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>HitSortingBinningZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>Defines spatial slice in Z</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MaxClusterSizeForMerge</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>3</code></td>
                <td>Defines the maximum number of adjacent hits which can be merged</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>N_eff</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>22</code></td>
                <td>Number of Effective electrons per pad in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PointResolutionPadPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.9</code></td>
                <td>Pad Phi Resolution constant in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PointResolutionRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.05</code></td>
                <td>R-Phi Resolution constant in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PointResolutionZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.4</code></td>
                <td>TPC Z Resolution Coefficent independent of diffusion</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>RejectCellID0</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>whether or not to use hits without proper cell ID (pad row)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SimTrkHitRelCollection</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>TPCTrackerHitRelations</code></td>
                <td>Name of TrackerHit SimTrackHit relation collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TPCLowPtCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>TPCLowPtCollection</code></td>
                <td>Name of the LowPt SimTrackerHit collection Produced by Mokka TPC Driver TPC0X</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TPCPadRowHitCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>TPCCollection</code></td>

      <div class="alg-card" data-name="DDPlanarDigiProcessor" data-lib="MarlinTrkProcessors" data-package="MarlinTrkProcessors">
        <div class="alg-card-header">
          <span class="alg-name">DDPlanarDigiProcessor</span>
          <span class="alg-card-right">
            <span class="alg-lib-badge">MarlinTrkProcessors</span>
            <span class="alg-card-toggle">&#9658;</span>
          </span>
        </div>
        <div class="alg-card-body">
          <p class="alg-description">DDPlanarDigiProcessor creates TrackerHits from SimTrackerHits, smearing their position and time according to the input parameters.The geoemtry of the surface is taken from the DDRec::Surface associated to the hit via the cellID</p>
          <table class="alg-props-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Parameter</th>
                <th>Type</th>
                <th>Default</th>
                <th>Description</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><code>CorrectTimesForPropagation</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Correct hit time for the propagation: radial distance/c (default: false)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ForceHitsOntoSurface</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Project hits onto the surface in case they are not yet on the surface (default: false)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>IsStrip</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>whether hits are 1D strip hits</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>MinimumEnergyPerHit</code></td>
                <td><code>double</code></td>
                <td><code>0</code></td>
                <td>Minimum Energy (in GeV!) to accept hits, other hits are ignored</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ResolutionT</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>-1</code></td>
                <td>resolution of time - either one per layer or one for all layers. if the single entry is negative, disable time smearing.</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ResolutionU</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>0.004</code></td>
                <td>resolution in direction of u - either one per layer or one for all layers</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>ResolutionV</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>0.004</code></td>
                <td>resolution in direction of v - either one per layer or one for all layers</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SimTrackHitCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>VXDCollection</code></td>
                <td>Name of the Input SimTrackerHit collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SimTrkHitRelCollection</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>VTXTrackerHitRelations</code></td>
                <td>Name of TrackerHit SimTrackHit relation collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SubDetectorName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>VXD</code></td>
                <td>Name of dub detector</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TimeWindowMax</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>1e+09</code></td>
                <td>Maximum time a hit must have after smearing to be accepted [ns] - either one per layer or one for all layers</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TimeWindowMin</code></td>
                <td><code>FloatVec</code></td>
                <td><code>-1e+09</code></td>
                <td>Minimum time a hit must have after smearing to be accepted [ns] - either one per layer or one for all layers</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TrackerHitCollectionName</code></td>
                <td><code>string</code></td>
                <td><code>VTXTrackerHits</code></td>
                <td>Name of the TrackerHit output collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>UseTimeWindow</code></td>
                <td><code>bool</code></td>
                <td><code>false</code></td>
                <td>Only accept hits with time (after smearing) within the specified time window (default: false)</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="alg-card" data-name="DDSpacePointBuilder" data-lib="MarlinTrkProcessors" data-package="MarlinTrkProcessors">
        <div class="alg-card-header">
          <span class="alg-name">DDSpacePointBuilder</span>
          <span class="alg-card-right">
            <span class="alg-lib-badge">MarlinTrkProcessors</span>

        <div class="alg-card-body">
          <p class="alg-description">DDSpacePointBuilder combine si-strip measurements into 3D spacepoints (1TrackerHitPlanar+1TrackHitPlanar = 1 TrackerHit), that can be used by reconstruction</p>

      <div class="alg-card" data-name="DDTPCDigiProcessor" data-lib="MarlinTrkProcessors" data-package="MarlinTrkProcessors">
        <div class="alg-card-header">
          <span class="alg-name">DDTPCDigiProcessor</span>
          <span class="alg-card-right">
            <span class="alg-lib-badge">MarlinTrkProcessors</span>
            <span class="alg-card-toggle">&#9658;</span>
          </span>
        </div>
        <div class="alg-card-body">
          <p class="alg-description">Produces TPC TrackerHit collection from SimTrackerHit collection, smeared in RPhi and Z. A search is made for adjacent hits on a pad row, if they are closer in z and r-phi than the steering parameters _doubleHitResRPhi (default value 2.0 mm) and _doubleHitResZ (default value 5.0 mm) they are considered to overlap. Clusters of hits smaller than _maxMerge (default value 3) are merged into a single tracker hit, with the position given as the average poision of the hits in phi and in z. Clusters which have _maxMerge hits or more are determined to be identifiable as multiple hits, and are not added to the tracker hit collection. This of course means that good hits caught up in a cluster of background hits will be lossed.</p>
          <table class="alg-props-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Parameter</th>
                <th>Type</th>
                <th>Default</th>
                <th>Description</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DiffusionCoeffRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.025</code></td>
                <td>R-Phi Diffusion Coefficent in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DiffusionCoeffZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.08</code></td>
                <td>Z Diffusion Coefficent in TPC</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DoubleHitResolutionRPhi</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>2</code></td>
                <td>Defines the minimum distance for two seperable hits in RPhi</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>DoubleHitResolutionZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>5</code></td>
                <td>Defines the minimum distance for two seperable hits in Z</td>
              </tr>

              </tr>

                <td><code>PointResolutionPadPhi</code></td>

              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>PointResolutionZ</code></td>
                <td><code>float</code></td>
                <td><code>0.4</code></td>
                <td>TPC Z Resolution Coefficent independent of diffusion</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>RejectCellID0</code></td>
                <td><code>int</code></td>
                <td><code>1</code></td>
                <td>whether or not to use hits without proper cell ID (pad row)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>SimTrkHitRelCollection</code></td>

                <td><code>TPCTrackerHitRelations</code></td>
                <td>Name of TrackerHit SimTrackHit relation collection</td>
              </tr>
              <tr>
                <td><code>TPCEndPlateModuleGapPhi</code></td>

              </tr>

<script>
(function () {
  var totalItems = 212;
  var totalPackages = 20;

  var searchInput = document.getElementById('alg-search');
  var statsEl = document.getElementById('alg-stats');
  var overview = document.getElementById('algorithm-overview');

  // Toggle package group collapse/expand
  overview.querySelectorAll('.alg-package-header').forEach(function (header) {
    header.addEventListener('click', function () {
      header.closest('.alg-package-group').classList.toggle('collapsed');
    });
  });

  // Toggle card expand/collapse
  overview.querySelectorAll('.alg-card-header').forEach(function (header) {
    header.addEventListener('click', function () {
      header.closest('.alg-card').classList.toggle('expanded');
    });
  });

  function debounce(fn, delay) {
    var timer;
    return function () {
      clearTimeout(timer);
      timer = setTimeout(fn, delay);
    };
  }

  function updateStats(visibleCards, visiblePackages) {
    statsEl.textContent =
      'Showing ' + visibleCards + ' of ' + totalItems +
      ' algorithms in ' + visiblePackages + ' packages';
  }

  function filterCards() {
    var query = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();
    var visibleCards = 0;

    overview.querySelectorAll('.alg-card').forEach(function (card) {
      if (!query) {
        card.style.display = '';
        visibleCards++;
        return;
      }
      var name = (card.dataset.name || '').toLowerCase();
      var lib  = (card.dataset.lib  || '').toLowerCase();
      var pkg  = (card.dataset.package || '').toLowerCase();
      var matches = name.indexOf(query) !== -1 ||
                    lib.indexOf(query)  !== -1 ||
                    pkg.indexOf(query)  !== -1;
      card.style.display = matches ? '' : 'none';
      if (matches) visibleCards++;
    });

    var visiblePackages = 0;
    overview.querySelectorAll('.alg-package-group').forEach(function (group) {
      var anyVisible = false;
      group.querySelectorAll('.alg-card').forEach(function (c) {
        if (c.style.display !== 'none') anyVisible = true;
      });
      group.style.display = anyVisible ? '' : 'none';
      if (anyVisible) visiblePackages++;
    });

    updateStats(visibleCards, visiblePackages);
  }

  searchInput.addEventListener('input', debounce(filterCards, 200));

  // URL hash deep-linking: #Name expands and scrolls to that card
  function handleHash() {
    var hash = decodeURIComponent(window.location.hash.slice(1));
    if (!hash) return;
    var target = null;
    overview.querySelectorAll('.alg-card').forEach(function (c) {
      if (c.dataset.name === hash) target = c;
    });
    if (!target) return;
    var group = target.closest('.alg-package-group');
    if (group) group.classList.remove('collapsed');
    target.classList.add('expanded');
    setTimeout(function () {
      target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
    }, 100);
  }

  window.addEventListener('hashchange', handleHash);
  handleHash();

  updateStats(totalItems, totalPackages);
})();
</script>
```
